        function trackOutboundLink(link, category, action) {
            try {
                ga('send', 'event', {
                    eventCategory: category,
                    eventAction: action
                });
            } catch (err) {
            }
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (link.target == "_blank") {
                    window.open(link.href, '_blank');
                } else {
                    document.location.href = link.href;
                }
            }, 100);
        }
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {

        $(".currentLanguage").on('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.keyCode === 13 || event.keyCode === 32 || (event.keyCode === 40 && !$('.languages').is(":visible"))) {
                $(this).click();
                return false;
            }
            if ((event.keyCode === 40 && $('.languages').is(":visible"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                $(".languages").find(".language").not("current").first().focus();
            }
            return true;
        });

        $('.currentLanguage').click(function () {
            var parent = $(this).closest('.languageSelectionWrapper');
            var languages = $('.languages');
            if (languages.is(":visible")) {
                parent.removeClass('open');
                languages.velocity("slideUp");
            } else {
                parent.addClass('open');
                languages.velocity("slideDown");
            }
        });

        $(".countries").find(".country.current").hide();
        $(".currentCountry").on('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.keyCode === 13 || event.keyCode === 32 || (event.keyCode === 40 && !$('.countries').is(":visible"))) {
                $(this).click();
                return false;
            }
            if ((event.keyCode === 40 && $('.countries').is(":visible"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                $(".countries").find(".country").not("current").first().focus();
            }
            return true;
        });

        $('.currentCountry').click(function () {
            var parent = $(this).closest('.countrySelectionWrapper');
            var countries = $('.countries');
            if (countries.is(":visible")) {
                parent.removeClass('open');
                countries.velocity("slideUp");
            } else {
                parent.addClass('open');
                countries.velocity("slideDown");
            }
        });
    });
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">

        var criteriaModel;
        $(document).ready(function() {

            var criteria = {
                SearchType: 'Normal',
                AvailType: '',
                IsReturnTrip: false,
                Adults: '2',
                Children: '3',
                Infants: '1',
                FareDesignator: '',
                HaveErrors: false,
                IsChangeBooking: false,
                Currency: 'COP',
                ConvertedCurrency: 'COP',
                OutFlightNumber: '',
                InFlightNumber: '',
                OutClassCode: '',
                InClassCode: '',
                ProductClass: '',
                Flights: [{"DepartureAirport":"BOG","ArrivalAirport":"CTG","DepartureDate":"\/Date(1541829600000)\/","DepartureDateString":"2018-11-10"}]
            };

            for (var i = 0; i < criteria.Flights.length; i++) {
                var flight = criteria.Flights[i];
                flight.DepartureDate = moment(flight.DepartureDate).toDate();
                if (flight.DepartureDateString !== undefined && flight.DepartureDateString !== null) {
                    var parsedDate = moment(flight.DepartureDateString, "YYYY-MM-DD").toDate();
                    if (parsedDate.getTime() !== flight.DepartureDate.getTime()) {
                        flight.DepartureDate = parsedDate;
                    }
                }
            }

            var options = {
                haveErrorsField: $("#LastSearch_HaveErrors"),
                criteria: criteria,
                departureDate: $('#DepartureDate'),
                returnDate: $('#ReturnDate'),
                language: 'en-co'
            };

            criteriaModel = new FlightCriteria(options);
        });
        </script>

                        CancelDialogText: "No"
                    }
                }
            };

            var controls = {
                bus: {
                    OneWay: $(".busOneWay"),
                    RoundTrip: $(".busRoundTrip"),
                    NoTransport: $(".busNoTransport"),
                    Selection: $(".busOptions"),
                    SelectionDiv: $(".busSelection"),

                    To: $(".busTravelTo"),

                },
                insurance: {
                    options: $(".radInsuranceOption")
                },
                baggage: {
                    upgradeBaggageSelectBox: $("select.selectBaggageUpgrade"),
                    protectBaggageCheckBox: $("#protectBaggage")
                },

                },

                },
                popups: $('#extras .fancybox')
            };

            var hasUsaAirport = false;

            var seatingOptions = {
                translation: translations.seat,
                changeBookingViewType: 'None',
                bookingHasReturnFlight: false,
                isOneway: true,
                passengerNumbersWithSpecialAssistance: [],
                specialAssistanceSsrsThatCanSelectSeat: ["ZLAG","ZBLN","ZDEA","ZPMR"]
                };

            window.seatingViewModel = new SeatingViewModel(seatingOptions);

            var seating = ezy.views.flight.seating();
            seating.init({
                translations: translations.seat,
                controls: controls.seat,
                changeBookingViewType: 'None',
                nrOfSeats: 5,
                seatVipPreSelected: false,
                hasPvip: false,
                selectedSeats: []
            }, window.seatingViewModel);

            var model = ezy.views.flight.extras();
            model.init({
                translations: translations,
                form: $("#extrasForm"),
                edit: $('#extras .edit'),
                rowAmount: $('.rowAmount'),
                totalExtras: $('.totalExtras'),
                bottomContainer: $('#extrasContinueButtonContainer'),
                validationMessages: {
                    travelInsuranceTermsAndConditions: 'I have read and accept'
                },
                validationElements:{
                    travelinsuranceTermsAndConditions: $('#chkTravelInsurance')
                },
                changeBookingViewType: '',
                hasPriviuosSeatReservations: false,
                hasUsaAirport: hasUsaAirport,
                controls: controls
            });

            model.doInit();
            model.setEvents();

            window.ExtrasViewModel = ezy.ExtrasViewModel();

            window.ExtrasViewModel.changeBookingViewType('None');
            window.ExtrasViewModel.StaffLoggedIn = false;

            window.ExtrasViewModel.Translations = {
                FailedToAddExtraError: "Could not be added.",
                FailedToRemoveExtraError: "Could not be removed.",
                ValidationSeatingIsRequiredText: "With VivaMax you have included the seat assignment service. Select the best seat!",

                SeatNotAllowedForInfant: "Seat is not allowed with infant.",
                NoThanksText: "No thanks.",
                StaffFreeBagOptionText: "Free bags for Staff",
                InfantNotAllowedPopup: {
                    AcceptButtonText: "Accept",

            };

            window.ExtrasViewModel.Translations.SeatingWarningPopUp = {
                AreYouSureYouDontWantSeating: "All passengers must select a chair. If the passenger is not selected, the system will assign a random one at no extra cost. We can not guarantee that you feel close to your friends or family.",

and Tobago"},{"Code":"TV","Name":"Tuvalu"},{"Code":"TW","Name":"Taiwan"},{"Code":"TZ","Name":"Tanzania"},{"Code":"UA","Name":"Ukraine"},{"Code":"UG","Name":"Uganda"},{"Code":"UM","Name":"United States Grenadines"},{"Code":"VE","Name":"Venezuela"},{"Code":"VG","Name":"British Virgin Islands"},{"Code":"VI","Name":"US Virgin Islands"},{"Code":"VN","Name":"Vietnam"},{"Code":"VU","Name":"Vanuatu"},{"Code":"WF","Name":"Wallis and Futuna Islands"},{"Code":"WS","Name":"Samoa"},{"Code":"YE","Name":"Yemen"},{"Code":"YT","Name":"Mayotte"},{"Code":"ZA","Name":"South Africa"},{"Code":"ZM","Name":"Zambia"},{"Code":"ZW","Name":"Zimbabwe"}];
                var creditCardOptions = [{"Name":"Visa","Code":"VI","MaxInstallments":36},{"Name":"Mastercard","Code":"MC","MaxInstallments":36},{"Name":"American Express","Code":"AX","MaxInstallments":32},{"Name":"Diners","Code":"DN","MaxInstallments":36}];

                inner.selectedCountry = ko.observable(window.AirlineCountryCode);
                inner.selectedState = ko.observable("");
                inner.selectedCreditCard = ko.observable("");
                inner.selectedInstallment = ko.observable(new Installment(1));

                inner.phoneNumberSelectorValue = ko.observable("");
                inner.phoneNumberSelectorValue.subscribe(function() {
                    inner.updatePhoneNumber();
                });

                inner.updatePhoneNumber = function() {
                    var phoneNumber = $("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_PhoneNumberSelector").intlTelInput("getNumber", window.intlTelInputUtils.numberFormat.NATIONAL);
                    inner.phoneNumber(phoneNumber.replace(/-/g, ""));
                    var countryData = $("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_PhoneNumberSelector").intlTelInput("getSelectedCountryData");
                    inner.phonePrefix(countryData ? countryData.dialCode : "");
                };

                inner.phoneNumber = ko.observable("");
                inner.phonePrefix = ko.observable("");

                inner.countries = ko.observableArray([]);
                inner.states = ko.observableArray([]);
                inner.creditCards = ko.observableArray([]);
                inner.installments = ko.observableArray([]);

                inner.skipPaymentUpdate = false;

                inner.enableVisaDebit = ko.observable(false);
                inner.enableInstallments = ko.observable(true);

                inner.countries = ko.utils.arrayMap(countries, function(item) {
                    return new Country(item);
                });

                inner.creditCards = ko.utils.arrayMap(creditCardOptions, function(item) {
                    return new CreditCard(item);
                });

                inner.selectedCreditCard.subscribe(function() {
                    inner.skipPaymentUpdate = true;
                    inner.setInstallments();
                    inner.skipPaymentUpdate = false;

                    $.publish('payment/ingenicoCreditCardPaymentUpdated');
                });

                inner.selectedInstallment.subscribe(function() {
                    if (!inner.skipPaymentUpdate) {
                        $.publish('payment/ingenicoCreditCardPaymentUpdated');
                    }
                });

                inner.setInstallments = function() {
                    var maxInstallments = 1;
                    $.each(creditCardOptions, function(index, element) {
                        if (element.Code === inner.selectedCreditCard()) {
                            maxInstallments = element.MaxInstallments;
                        }
                    });

                    if (maxInstallments === 1) {
                        inner.installments([new Installment(1)]);
                        return;
                    }

                    var installments = [];
                    var i = 1;
                    for (i = 1; i <= maxInstallments; i++) {
                        installments.push(new Installment(i));
                    }
                    inner.installments(installments);
                };

                inner.showStates = ko.observable(false);
                inner.selectedCountry.subscribe(function () {
                    try {
                            var country = inner.selectedCountry();
                            ezy.defaultAjax("/FCPassengerDetailsPart/GetStates", { country: country }, inner.setCountryStates, inner.failedGettingCountryStates);
                            $("#CreditCardPayment_StateDrop").trigger("change.select2");

                    } catch (e) {
                        console.log("Error in selectedCountry.subscribe ex:" + e);
                    }
                });

                inner.showStates = ko.observable(false);
                inner.setCountryStates = function (states) {
                    inner.states(states);
                    inner.showStates(states.length > 0 && (inner.selectedCountry() === "US" || inner.selectedCountry() === "CA"));
                    if (inner.selectedCountry() === "US" || inner.selectedCountry() === "CA") {
                        $("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_Zip").rules("add", {
                            required: true,
                            messages: {
                                required: "You need to enter a zip code"
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_Zip").rules("remove", "required");
                    }
                };

                inner.failedGettingCountryStates = function () {
                    console.log("Failed getting states for selected country.");
                };
                inner.setSelectedCountry = function(countryToSelect) {
                    //if (countryToSelect) {
                    //    countryToSelect = inner.countries[0].name;
                    //}

                    //var country = $.grep(inner.countries, function(e) { return e.name === countryToSelect; });
                    //if (country.length === 1) {
                    //    inner.selectedCountry(country[0]);
                    //}

                    //$("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_CountryDrop").trigger("change.select2");
                };

                inner.setSelectedState = function(stateToSelect) {
                    //var state = $.grep(inner.states(), function(e) { return e.name === stateToSelect; });
                    //if (state.length >= 1) {
                    //    inner.selectedState(state[0]);
                    //} else {
                    //    inner.selectedState("");
                    //}

                    //$("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_StateDrop").trigger("change.select2");
                };

                return inner;
            };

            var creditCardViewModel = new viewModel();
            ko.applyBindings(creditCardViewModel, document.getElementById("ingenico-creditcard-payment"));
            creditCardViewModel.selectedCountry.valueHasMutated();
            //creditCardViewModel.selectedCountry("CO");
            window.ingenicoCreditCardViewModel = creditCardViewModel;

            $("#IngenicoCreditCardPayment_PhoneNumberSelector").on("countrychange", function(e, countryData) {
                window.ingenicoCreditCardViewModel.updatePhoneNumber();
            });

        });
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function() {
            var Country = function(item) {
                var inner = {};
                inner.name = item.Text;
                inner.code = item.Value;
                return inner;
            };

            var viewModel = function() {
                var inner = {};
                var countries = [{"Selected":false,"Text":"Brasil","Value":"BR"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Canada","Value":"CA"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Chile","Value":"CL"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Colombia","Value":"CO"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Costa Rica","Value":"CR"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Ecuador","Value":"EC"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Mexico","Value":"MX"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Peru","Value":"PE"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Portugal","Value":"PT"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"España","Value":"ES"},{"Selected":false,"Text":"Estados Unidos","Value":"US"}];
                inner.selectedCountry = ko.observable();

                inner.countries = ko.observableArray([]);
                $.each(countries, function () {
                    var country = new Country(this);
                    inner.countries.push(country);
                });

                inner.selectedCountryCode = ko.computed(function() {
                    var code = inner.selectedCountry() !== undefined ? inner.selectedCountry() : "";
                    return code;
                });

                return inner;
            };

            var safetyPayCashViewModel = new viewModel();
            ko.applyBindings(safetyPayCashViewModel, document.getElementById("safetyPayCash"));
            window.safetyPayCashViewModel = safetyPayCashViewModel;
        });
    </script>

        <script>
            function loadBoxeverScript(url, callback) {
                if (window.LoadBoxeverScripts) {
                    var script = document.createElement("script");
                    script.type = "text/javascript";

                    if (script.readyState) { //IE
                        script.onreadystatechange = function () {
                            if (script.readyState === "loaded" ||
                                script.readyState === "complete") {
                                script.onreadystatechange = null;
                                if (typeof callback === "function") {
                                    callback();
                                }
                            }
                        };
                    } else { //Others
                        script.onload = function () {
                            if (typeof callback === "function") {
                                callback();
                            }
                        };
                    }

                    script.src = url;
                    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
                } else {
                    if (typeof callback === "function") {
                        callback();
                    }
                }
            }
